<h1>Magic Online Privacy Policy</h1>
<p class="posted-in">
      Posted in      <strong class="breadcrumb-no-link">Magic Online New Players</strong>
      on June 15, 2016    </p>
<!-- BEGIN :: ARTICLE -->
<article>
<div class="article-header">
<div class="author">
<img alt="" src="https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_author.jpg"/>
<p>By Wizards of the Coast</p>

<html><body><div>
<p><strong><em>MAGIC ONLINE</em> PRIVACY POLICY</strong></p>
<p><strong>UPDATED <span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441">October 22, 2020 </span></span></span></span></span></span></span></strong></p>
<hr/> 
<h2 style="margin-top: 32px; margin-bottom: 13px; text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="line-height:107%"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style="font-size:18.0pt"><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441"><span style="text-transform:uppercase">1. INTRODUCTION</span></span></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></h2>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441">Wizards of the Coast LLC (“Wizards, “we,” “our,” or “us”) has adopted this privacy policy ("Privacy Policy") to explain how we collect, store, and use your information. This Privacy Policy applies to all online service locations operated or controlled by Wizards that post a link to this Privacy Policy, including our website at </span></span><span style="color:black"><a href="http://www.wizards.com/" target="_blank"><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'><span style="color:#1dcbeb">www.wizards.com</span></span></a></span><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441">, our apps, and our customer service program, and all features, contents, and other services operated or controlled by Wizards through such online service locations (collectively, the “Service”). This Privacy Policy does not apply to our information collection activities outside of the Service (unless otherwise stated below or at the time of collection).</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441">By using the Service, you agree to our </span></span><span style="color:black"><a href="http://company.wizards.com/legal/terms-use"><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'><span style="color:#1dcbeb"><span style="text-decoration:none"><span style="text-underline:none">Terms of Use</span></span></span></span></b></a></span><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441"> and consent to our processing of information as described in this Privacy Policy. If you do not agree and consent, please do not use the Service.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:16px; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441">If you are a parent or guardian of a child, please review the section entitled Children’s Information below.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:16px; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441">If you are a California resident or data subject in Europe, please see the “Additional Disclosures for California Residents” or “Additional Disclosures for Data Subjects in Europe” sections.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-bottom:16px; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441">If you have any questions or wish to exercise your rights and choices, please contact us as set out in the “Contact Us” section.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<h2 style="margin-top: 32px; margin-bottom: 13px; text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="line-height:107%"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style="font-size:18.0pt"><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441"><span style="text-transform:uppercase">2. ESRB PRIVACY CERTIFIED</span></span></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></h2>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441">The ESRB certification seals shown on our Service confirm that Wizards is a valid licensee, and participating member, of the</span></span><span style="color:black"><a href="http://www.esrb.org/privacy/faq.aspx#10" target="_blank"><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'><span style="color:#1dcbeb"> Entertainment Software Rating Board’s Privacy Certified Program</span></span></a></span><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441"> (“ESRB Privacy Certified”). To help protect your privacy, we have voluntarily undertaken this privacy initiative and have had all areas of our Service where this Privacy Policy is posted reviewed and certified by ESRB Privacy Certified to meet established online information collection, use, and disclosure practices. As a licensee of this program, we are subject to audits of our Service and other enforcement and accountability mechanisms administered independently by the ESRB.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<h2 style="margin-top: 32px; margin-bottom: 13px; text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style="line-height:107%"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style="font-size:18.0pt"><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441"><span style="text-transform:uppercase">3. INFORMATION COLLECTION</span></span></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></h2>
<ol><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Information You Provide</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ol><p style="margin-bottom:16px; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441">Wizards collects information you provide directly via the Service. The data we collect may include data that identifies you personally (whether alone or in combination). The categories of information we have collected in the last 12 months include the following:</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Contact Data. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>We collect your first and last name, email address, postal address, telephone number and other similar contact data.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul><p style="margin-bottom:16px; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'> </span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Credentials. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>We collect passwords, password hints and similar security information used for authentication and account access.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul><p style="margin-left:48px; text-align:justify"> </p>
<ul><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Demographic Data. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>We collect demographic information such as about your age, birth date, gender and country.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul><p style="margin-left:48px; text-align:justify"> </p>
<ul><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Payment Data. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>We collect data necessary to process your payment if you make purchases, such as your payment instrument, shipping address and transaction numbers.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul><p style="margin-left:48px; text-align:justify"> </p>
<ul><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Profile Data. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>We collect your username, interests, favorites, gamer data and other profile information.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul><p style="margin-left:48px; text-align:justify"> </p>
<ul><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Contacts. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>We collect data about your contacts if you choose to match with your contacts on the Service or invite your contacts to join the Service.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul><p style="text-align:justify"> </p>
<ul><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Content. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>We collect the content of messages you send to us, such as feedback and product reviews you write, or questions and information you provide for customer support. We also collect the content of your communications as necessary to provide you with the services you use. For example, if you chat with another user through the Service, we need to collect the content of that chat to display it to you and the other user as you direct.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul><p style="margin-bottom:16px; text-align:justify"> </p>
<p style="margin-bottom:16px; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441">Wizards collects data from you at various points on the Service, including as described below:</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Account Registration. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>To register an account with Wizards, you must, at a minimum, provide your date of birth, location, email, a username and password. To participate in other Wizards offerings, such as organized play, you may be required to provide your first name and last name, city, country, postal code, gender, email address, password, username and screen name.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Profile. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>For certain parts of our Service, your personal profile (“Your Profile”) will be automatically populated with the screen name you provided at registration. Where applicable, the information in Your Profile, including any information or content you voluntarily add to Your Profile such as first and last name and images you upload, will be made public by default. To change Your Profile privacy settings for these parts of the Service, log in to</span><span style="color:black"><a href="https://accounts.wizards.com/" target="_blank"><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'><span style="color:#1dcbeb"> accounts.wizards.com</span></span></a></span><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'> and go to Your My Account tab then click “Edit Public Profile &amp; Settings.” In this section, you may also change Your Profile information, who can view your page and activity, and who can contact you on these parts of the Service, as well as control how we communicate with you. Your Profile for these parts of the Service will be searchable by screen name, and you can change the visibility of Your Profile by de-selecting the “Profile is visible to other users” and “Profile is searchable” boxes in Privacy Settings. Please note: The photo you selected (you are not required to upload a personal photo) as your avatar and your screen name for these parts of the Service will always display on your page, posts, and in search results. You are responsible for any information and content you choose to make public either through Your Profile, or by posting on the Service. Profile settings and data processing may differ based on the part of the Service you are using.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Message Boards, Forums, Blogs, and Chats. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Wizards provides message boards, blogs, chats, and other public forums on the Service for exchanging information and communicating with other users. Please note that any information, user content, or any other materials that you post on our Service, including any information from Your Profile, where applicable, that you choose to make public, may be available for any user of the Service to read, and are therefore no longer private and may be disclosed by third parties. If you post information, materials, or other content on the Service, you are providing information that can be collected and used by others that you do not know, for their own purposes, including the distribution of unsolicited communications.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Online Stores. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Visitors purchasing goods and services through our Service will need to provide valid Payment Data, in addition to Contact Data such as name, mailing address, phone number and email address.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Promotions. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>To participate in some of our sweepstakes, contests, surveys, or other promotions (“Promotions”), you may be asked to provide an email address or screen name, so that we can let you know if you won a prize. We may also request your name and home address in order to send you products or information by regular mail.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Customer Service. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>When you contact customer service you may be asked to provide us with information such as your name, telephone number, address and email. We collect this information as part of our customer service efforts and it is used to confirm your identity, respond to your inquiry or comments, for training purposes, and to assist us in providing better products and services.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Wizards Play Network. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Participants, including store owners and event organizers, have the opportunity to sign up with the Wizards Play Network in order to run organized play events. You must provide certain information to be eligible to participate in organized play.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Job Postings. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Our Service allows for the online submission of resumes, employment and education history, transcript, writing samples, and references which are used solely for the purpose of accepting and evaluating candidate submissions for job postings.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul><p style="margin-left:48px; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'><span style="color:#454441">Online Surveys. </span></span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441">In order to improve the user experience at our Service, we may employ online surveys for visitors to volunteer information about themselves and provide us feedback about why they visit our Service and what we can do to make them better.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p style="margin-left:48px; text-align:justify"> </p>
<p style="margin-bottom:16px; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441">Whatever the activity may be, we will only collect information to the extent it is reasonably necessary to fulfill your requests and our legitimate business objectives. If you do not want to submit certain information when requested, you may not be able to access certain areas on our Service or take advantage of certain features of our Service. You may choose to voluntarily submit other information to us through the Service that we do not request, and, in such instances, you are solely responsible for such information.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ol start="2"><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Information Collected Automatically</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ol><p style="margin-bottom:16px; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441">We automatically collect information when you use our Service. The categories of information we have automatically collected in the last 12 months include the following:</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Service Use Data. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>We collect data about the features you use, the products or services you view and purchase, the time of day you browse, information regarding your interaction with the Service, and the web pages you visit.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Game-</span></b><b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Related Data</span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>. We collect data about your use of games made available through the Service (“Game-related Data”). Game-related Data includes information about your game preferences, participation, performance and achievements in the game, your frequency of play, etc. </span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Device, Connectivity, and Configuration Data. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>We collect data about the type of device or browser you use, your device’s operating software, your regional and language settings, and other similar information. This also includes IP address, MAC address, mobile Ad Ids (e.g., IDFA or AAID), and other device identifiers.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Location Data. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>We collect data about your location, which can be precise or imprecise. Precise location data can be Global Navigation Satellite System (GNSS) data (e.g., GPS), as well as data identifying nearby cell towers and Wi-Fi hotspots. We collect precise location data when you enable location-based products or features. Imprecise location data includes, for example, a location derived from your IP address or data that indicates where you are located with less precision, such as at a city or postal code level.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Video Data</span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>. Certain of our games may allow you to activate the camera on your device and broadcast video of your gameplay to other players within the game. For example, when you use SpellTable to play Magic: The Gathering, you may have the option to activate the camera on your device in order to show the physical cards to other players within the game. If you activate the camera, we will only access and collect video through the camera for the purpose of providing this functionality to you. We will not use the video for any other purpose or share the video with anyone outside of our Service, except where necessary for us to comply with our legal obligations, to protect our rights or those of anyone else, or where otherwise instructed by you or to facilitate organized play activities. In addition, you can disable your camera at any time through your device settings. Notwithstanding the above, we may use non-video data collected in connection with your use of the camera for additional purposes such as data analytics and improving our internal ad servers or as otherwise in accordance with this Privacy Policy. </span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul><p style="margin-bottom:16px; text-align:justify"> </p>
<p style="margin-bottom:16px; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441">We use various current – and later – developed technologies to collect this data (“Tracking Technologies”), including the following:</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Log Files. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Log-files are files that record website activity and gather statistics about web users' browsing habits. These entries help Wizards determine (among other things) how many and how often users have visited our Service, which pages they've visited, and other similar data. We also use the log file entries for our internal marketing and demographic studies, so we can constantly improve the online services we provide you.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul><ul><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Cookies</span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>. Cookies are pieces of information placed on your device when you visit a website that act as a unique tag to identify your browser. We use "cookies" to enhance your experience at our Service and to help us understand how you interact with our Service. For example, a cookie may allow us to remember certain things based on your IP address, such as the time and duration of your visits, how you navigated through our content, and where you exited a particular site. To learn more about how we use cookies, please visit our </span><span style="color:black"><a href="http://company.wizards.com/legal/cookies"><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'><span style="color:#1dcbeb"><span style="text-decoration:none"><span style="text-underline:none">Cookie Policy</span></span></span></span></b></a></span><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Clear GIFs</span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>. Clear GIFs, sometimes called “pixel tags,” or “web beacons” are file objects, usually a graphic image such as a transparent one pixel-by-one-pixel GIF, that are placed on a web page, advertisement, or in an email message. The GIF may tell us the IP address of the device that fetched our page, the URL of the page the GIF is on, the time the page was viewed, the type of browser used, and it can also identify a previously set cookie value, and how and where a user accessed a website. We may use this information to count visitors across our Service and understand how they navigate and use our Service.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Location-Identifying Technologies</span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>. GPS, WiFi, Bluetooth, and other location-aware technologies may be used to determine your device’s location, sometimes precisely. Location data may be used for purposes such as verifying your device’s location and delivering or restricting relevant content and advertising based on that location.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Voice Processing Technologies</span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>. Voice processing technologies collect audio through the microphone on your device to effectuate an instruction or request by you. We only collect audio with your consent. We only maintain the audio long enough to complete your instruction or request and then immediately delete it. We may use non-audio data associated with the collection for additional purposes such as data analytics.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>App-Specific Technologies</span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>. Our apps include app-specific technologies, such as SDKs and APIs provided by third parties. An SDK is code embedded in an app that sends information about your use to a server and is in effect the app version of a GIF. The information collected through such technologies often includes your mobile Ad Id.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul><p style="margin-left:24px; text-align:justify"> </p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441">For further information on how we use Tracking Technologies and your rights and choices regarding them, please see the sections entitled <b><span style="border:none windowtext 1.0pt; padding:0in">Social Media and Technology Integrations </span></b>and <b><span style="border:none windowtext 1.0pt; padding:0in">Your Rights and Choices</span></b>.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<ol><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Information Shared in the Last 12 Months</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>

<p style="margin-bottom:16px; text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><span style="color:#454441">Wizards shares information about you in accordance with the practices described in this Privacy Policy. The categories of entities to whom we disclosed information in the last 12 months include the following:</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ul><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Service Providers. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Wizards shares information about you with entities that process the information on our behalf (“Service Providers”). Service Providers assist us with operating our Service and provide us with other services such as organized play, community operations, online product fulfillment, prize payments, email services, marketing and promotional services, data analytics, and technical support. Also, if you make a purchase on the Service, your Payment Data may be processed by a payment processing Service Provider as necessary to complete your purchase (for example, to process your credit card). These Service Providers are contractually prohibited from using your information about you for any purpose other than to provide this assistance, and they agree to maintain the confidentiality, security and integrity of information they receive from us. We may, however, permit Service Providers to use aggregate information that does not identify you or de-identified information for any purposes except as prohibited by applicable law. We share the following categories of information with Service Providers: Contact Data, Payment Data, Credentials, Demographic Data, Profile Data, Contacts, and Content.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul><ul><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Vendors.</span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'> We share information with vendors, including analytics and advertising technology companies. Vendors may act as our Service Providers, or in certain contexts, independently decide how to process your information. For more information on advertising and analytics, see the section entitled <b><span style="border:none windowtext 1.0pt; padding:0in">Advertising and Analytics</span></b> below. For Vendors, we share the following categories of information with vendors: Contact Data, Credentials, and Profile Data</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul><ul><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Affiliates. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Wizards shares information with its related entities including its parent and sister companies. For example, we may share your information with our affiliates for customer support, marketing, or technical operations and such information includes: Contact Data, Credentials, Payment Data, and Profile Data.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul><ul><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Partners. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>We share information with our partners in connection with offering you co-branded services, selling or distributing our products, tournament and organized play activities, or engaging in joint marketing activities. For example, we may share information about you with a retailer for purposes of providing you with product support including Contact Data, Credentials, and Profile Data.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul><ul><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Tournament and Organized Play. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>If you engage in organized play, your full name, DCI number, city, state, nationality, username and email will be accessible by authorized tournament organizers, retail locations that are part of the Wizards Play Network, members of the Wizards’ community that are adjudicating organized play events, and prize fulfillment Service Providers. These parties are independent of Wizards, but they are contractually prohibited from using your information for any other purpose than that for which it was provided to them, and they agree to maintain the confidentiality, security and integrity of information they receive from us. Your information may also be disclosed to members of the Wizards’ community who are engaged in investigating violations of tournament rules and the Code of Conduct. Additionally, your full name, city, and country may appear in online leaderboards and organized play event results. Video Data may also be available to tournament organizers and retail locations that are part of the Wizards Play Network if you participate in organized play activities through SpellTable.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Promotions. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Our Promotions may be jointly sponsored or offered by other entities. If you voluntarily choose to enter a Promotion, we share information as set out in the official rules that govern the Promotion as well as for administrative purposes and as required by law (e.g., on a winners list). By entering, you agree to the official rules that govern that Promotion, and may, except where prohibited by applicable law, allow the sponsor and/or other parties to use your name, voice and/or likeness in advertising or marketing materials. We share the following information categories with promotional partners: Contact Data, Profile Data, and Content.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
<li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Facilitating Requests. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>We share information at your request or direction, such as when you choose to share information with a social network about your activities on the Service or link your Wizards account to gaming platforms (such as Steam or Twitch). Such disclosures include: Contact Data, Credentials, Profile Data, Contacts, and Content.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
</ul><p style="margin-left:48px; text-align:justify"> </p>

<ul><li style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:11pt"><span style="background:white"><span style="color:#454441"><span style="line-height:normal"><span style="tab-stops:list .5in"><span style="vertical-align:baseline"><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><b><span style='border:none windowtext 1.0pt; font-family:"Arial",sans-serif; padding:0in'>Merger or Acquisition. </span></b><span style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>In the event of, or during negotiations of, an actual or proposed merger, acquisition, reorganization, bankruptcy, or other similar event, your information, including personal data, may be shared with Wizards' successors or assigns or other third parties involved in the event. In the event of a merger or acquisition, we may share the following categories of information: Contact Data, Credentials, Demographic Data, Payment Data, Profile Data, Contacts, and Content.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>

We may also share your information in connection with an investigation of fraud, harassment, intellectual property infringements, or other activity that is illegal, a violation of our policies, or may expose you or us to legal liability. We may also share your information to protect the rights, property, life, health, security and safety of us, the Service or any third party. Such disclosures may include Contact Data, Payment Data, Credentials, Demographic Data, Profile Data, Contacts and Content.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></li>
